In Row 1, enter these headers (exactly): pgsql Copy Edit Timestamp | Name | Email | Address | Age | Gender | Password 2Ô∏è‚É£ Create Google Apps Script In your Sheet, click Extensions ‚Üí Apps Script. Delete any code in the file and replace it with this: javascript Copy Edit function doPost(e) { var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getActiveSheet(); var data = e.parameter; sheet.appendRow([ new Date(), data.name, data.email, data.address, data.age, data.gender, data.password ]); return ContentService.createTextOutput("Success").setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.TEXT); } 3Ô∏è‚É£ Deploy as Web App Click Deploy ‚Üí Manage Deployments. Click Create Deployment. Select Web App. Set: Description: Anything (e.g., ‚ÄúSign-Up Form‚Äù) Execute as: Me Who has access: Anyone Click Deploy. You said: Script function not found: doGet ChatGPT said: Ah, that‚Äôs a common little hiccup with Google Apps Script. The error is because the form is sending a POST request, but Google‚Äôs default behavior sometimes expects a GET request unless we set it up right. Let‚Äôs fix it properly so it works with your form submission: üîÑ Replace Your Entire Apps Script with This Final Working Version: javascript Copy Edit function doPost(e) { var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getActiveSheet(); var data = e.parameter; sheet.appendRow([ new Date(), data.name, data.email, data.address, data.age, data.gender, data.password ]); return ContentService.createTextOutput("Success"); } function doGet(e) { return ContentService.createTextOutput("GET request received. This is what we‚Äôll do here üëá üìù Final Working Sign-Up Form Code (AJAX Submit + Clean Redirect) Replace everything inside the <div class="form-section">...</div> in your signup/index.html file with this: html Copy Edit <div class="form-section"> <form id="signupForm"> <label for="name">Full Name</label> <input type="text" id="name" name="name" required> <label for="email">Email Address</label> <input type="email" id="email" name="email" required> <label for="address">Address</label> <input type="text" id="address" name="address" required> <label for="age">Age</label> <input type="number" id="age" name="age" required> <label for="gender">Gender</label> <select id="gender" name="gender" required> <option value="Male">Male</option> <option value="Female">Female</option> <option value="Other">Other</option> <option value="Prefer not to say">Prefer not to say</option> </select> <label for="password">Password</label> <input type="password" id="password" name="password" required> <button type="submit" class="submit-button">Sign Up - KABOOM!</button> </form> </div> <script> const form = document.getElementById('signupForm'); const scriptURL = 'https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbydIlQsmnDDIeJY9xYkpXwdcmZ6NB-cEkatGZRA775wAbBGDpWgrICNWjfOEb9LJRPj/exec'; form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); // Stop the default submission behavior const formData = new FormData(form); fetch(scriptURL, { method: 'POST', body: formData, }) .then(response => { if (response.ok) { window.location.href = 'https://nerdyprints.co.uk/thankyou/'; } else { alert('Something went wrong. Please try again.'); } }) .catch(error => { alert('An error occurred. Please try again later.'); console.error('Form submission error:', error); }); }); </script> üöÄ Why This Will Solve Your Problem No redirecting to the script URL in the browser anymore. Data is sent using JavaScript (AJAX). You are redirected only when the data is successfully submitted. No more Google iframe issues‚Äîthis is how most modern forms work. ‚úÖ Next Steps Replace the form section in your signup/index.html. Commit the changes to GitHub. Privacy Policy

Who We Are

Nerdy Prints is an online store offering custom-designed fandom merchandise. Our website is https://nerdyprints.co.uk.

What Data We Collect

When you sign up or place an order, we collect the following data:

  • Full Name
  • Email Address
  • Postal Address
  • Age
  • Gender
  • Password (encrypted)

Why We Collect Your Data

We collect this data to:

  • Create and manage your account
  • Process and fulfill your orders
  • Provide customer support
  • Send you important updates about your orders and account

Where Your Data Is Stored

Your data is securely stored in a Google Sheet accessed only by authorized Nerdy Prints personnel.

Who We Share Your Data With

We do not sell or share your personal data with third parties. We may share necessary details with our printing and shipping partners (e.g., Printful) solely to fulfill your orders.

Your Rights

You have the right to:

  • Request a copy of your data
  • Request corrections to your data
  • Request that we delete your data

To exercise your rights, please contact us at yourfandomyourstyle@gmail.com.

Contact Us

If you have any questions about this policy, please contact us at yourfandomyourstyle@gmail.com.

© 2025 Nerdy Prints. All rights reserved.

Here‚Äôs how it works conceptually: 1. Understanding the Current Setup Right now, your customize page is pulling data from your Printful store‚Äôs sync products and sync variants, which only gives: Product Name Thumbnail Image Variants (like size, color) Retail Price But it does not provide full descriptions or sizing info. 2. Combining Sync Product with Catalog Product Every Sync Product is based on a Catalog Product in Printful. You need to: Extract the catalog_product_id from your sync variant data. Each sync_variant includes product.id ‚Üí This is the Catalog Product ID. Use that product.id in another API request: javascript Copy Edit const catalogResponse = await fetch(`https://api.printful.com/products/${catalogProductId}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer YOUR_PRINTFUL_API_KEY' } }); const catalogData = await catalogResponse.json(); Now you get full description, size guide, and other details from catalogData.result. 4. You said: Response should not include unneeded headers: content-security-policy, x-xss-protection Response should not include unneeded headers: x-xss-protection Security Response should include 'x-content-type-options' header. The 'Expires' header should not be used, 'Cache-Control' should be preferred. The 'X-Frame-Options' header should not be used. A similar effect, with more consistent support and stronger checks, can be achieved with the 'Content-Security-Policy' header and 'frame-ancestors' directive. Other An element doesn't have an autocomplete attribute CSS inline styles should not be used, move styles to an external CSS file is the issue im getting while signing in ChatGPT said: These issues are mostly security recommendations and best practices for web development. Let‚Äôs break them down and handle each one: üîí 1. Security Headers Explanation & Fixes The headers mentioned are HTTP response headers. These aren't part of your HTML file; they come from the server (GitHub Pages or Netlify) when serving your website. Here‚Äôs what each means: Header Problem Solution Content-Security-Policy (CSP) Extra, possibly unnecessary Usually fine, but you can customize it later. X-XSS-Protection Old header, no longer needed Can be safely ignored. X-Content-Type-Options Missing nosniff is recommended You can add this via Netlify/Hosting settings later. Expires vs. Cache-Control Expires is outdated, Cache-Control is preferred. Can be ignored unless you handle advanced caching. X-Frame-Options Deprecated, Content-Security-Policy with frame-ancestors recommended. You can configure this later in Netlify/host settings. ‚úÖ What You Need To Do Right Now IGNORE these for now. They are server-side improvements and won‚Äôt break your login or website. Later: If you host on Netlify, you can set response headers like this in your netlify.toml file: toml Copy Edit [[headers]] for = "/*" [headers.values] X-Content-Type-Options = "nosniff" Content-Security-Policy = "frame-ancestors 'self'" Cache-Control = "public, max-age=3600" This is not urgent‚Äîjust polish for later. üìù 2. Autocomplete Missing on Inputs Browsers like when you tell them what kind of data you‚Äôre asking for, like: html Copy Edit üî• Fix for Sign-Up & Login Pages Add autocomplete like this in both forms: Sign-Up Page Example html Copy Edit Login Page Example html Copy Edit üé® 3. CSS Inline Styles Warning This is just a ‚Äúbest practice‚Äù suggestion, not an error. It‚Äôs saying: Move your
